#Identifier to uniquely specify a patient.	Tumor Registry ICD-O-3 Behavior Code	Derived Grade or Differentiation of Tumor	Histology Category	Histology	Indicates whether patient received neoadjuvant chemotherapy or radiation therapy before pathologic stage diagnosis	Indicates whether stage IV patient had distant metastases at time of cancer diagnosis.	Stage at Diagnosis	Indicates whether a distant adrenal metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant bone metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant brain metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant liver metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant lung metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant lymph metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant pleura metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant subcutaneous tissue metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Indicates whether a distant other site metastasis was identified at diagnosis.  Populated for Stage IV patients only.  	Year of Birth	Indication of Spanish/Hispanic origin of the patient; this data element maps to the NAACCR v16 #190. For institutions not collecting Spanish/Hispanic origin, submit a null in this category for all patients.	The primary race recorded for the patient; this data element maps to the NAACCR v16 #160. For institutions collecting more than one race category, this should be the primary race. For institutions not collecting race, submit a null in this category for all patients.	The sex code for the patient; this data element maps to the NAACCR v16 #220.	Center of Sequencing	Number of invasive and non-invasive/in situ cancer diagnoses ever experienced by the patient	Number of BPC Project cancers that were identified for a patient	The total number of cancer-directed drug regimens, including anti-neoplastic, immunotherapy, and hormone therapy that the patient has ever received for any cancer diagnosis	The total number of imaging scans reviewed starting in the month/year of the BPC Project cancer diagnosis	The number of CT imaging scans reviewed, starting in the month/year of the BPC Project cancer diagnosis	The number of MRI imaging scans reviewed, starting in the month/year of the BPC Project cancer diagnosis	The number of PET or PET-CT imaging scans reviewed, starting in the month/year of the BPC Project cancer diagnosis	The number of pathology reports starting in the month/year of the BPC Project cancer diagnosis	The number of medical oncologist assessments curated starting in the month/year of the BPC Project cancer diagnosis	The number of tumor marker results that were curated	Number of Tumor Marker CA19-9 Results	Number of Tumor Marker CEA Results
